ARIE 1927-1928 [vol. 050]


APPENDIX A.


List of copper-plates examined during the year 1927-28.


ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/1 (page )
Placement
The Raja Saheb of Sandur, through the Political Agent.
Dynasty
Vijayanagara
King
Kṛishṇarāyadēva
Date
Śaka 1210 (wrong), Sarvadhāri, Vaiśākha, śu. 13, Monday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
The writing looks quite modern. Purports to be a record executed during the reign of the Pradhānapaṇḍita Sāḷava Apaji-Panta in the presence of the assembly of several persons, making a gift of land to a carpenter named Rāmōju, son of Dēvōju. The grant is evidently a forgery.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/2 (page )
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1740, Bahudhānya.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inserittions.
Remarks
Registers the confirmation of the boundaries of Sāṇḍūru-jahāgīru by Thomas Munro Baha-dūr, made in the time of Śiva-Rao Hindu-Rao Ghōrpaḍe.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/3 (page )
Placement
The Trustee of the Śri-Mūkām-bikā temple at Kollūru, Coondapoor taluk, South Kanara district.
Dynasty
Keḷadi
King
Vīrabhadra-Nāyaka
Date
Śaka 1565, Sva-bhānu, Kārttika, śu. 15.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inserittions.
Remarks
Registers a grant of the income of two villages named Koḷambaḷike-Rāḍigrāma in Kabu-nāḍa-sīme and Vaḷarūra-[va]ṭa in Niru-ḷanāḍa-sīme by the king, for worship, offerings and lamps to the goddess Mūkām-bikā and the subsidiary deities in the temple at Kollūru.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/4 (page )
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Do.
Date
Śaka 1565, Chitrabhānu, Phālguṇa, śu. 15.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inserittions.
Remarks
Records the remission of taxes on some lands in Hose-ūru by the king in favour of the temple of Mūkāmbikā-Amma at Kollūru for its requirements, in return for a lump sum of 200 varāhas received from a certain Śāntayya.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/5 (page )
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Veṅkaṭappa-Nāyaka
Date
Śaka 1550, Prabhava, Āshāḍha, śu. 15.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inserittions.
Remarks
Records the allotment of the village Kaḷasi in Jālida-sīme by the king to a certain Chik-kaṁna, for a lump sum of 330 varāhas, for the maintenance out of its annual income in paddy, of a feeding choultry established by the donor in a suburb of Dharmapuri in Haṁnarada-sīme. The management was vested in the temple of Mūkāmbikā.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/6 (page )
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Vīrabhadra-Nāyaka
Date
Śaka 1564 Vṛisha, Vaiśākha, śu. 10.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inserittions.
Remarks
Registers the allotment of the annual income from certain specified sources in a few villages amounting to 1,002 varāhas and the income in kind from 9 other villages by the king, for the maintenance of the daily worship and offerings in the temple of Mūkāmbikā at Kollūru.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/6A (page )
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Do.
Date
Śaka 1563 (wrong), Vṛisha, Vai-śākha, śu. 10.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inserittions.
Remarks
Seems to be an incorrect copy of the above record, but left incomplete.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/7 (page 6)
Placement
P.Ayyasvami Gurukkal, Anaimalai, Pollachi taluk, Coimbatore district.
Dynasty
Mysore
King
Kṛishṇarāja-Voḍeya, ‘ruling from Śrīraṅgapaṭṭaṇa’.
Date
Śaka 1685, Kali 4864, Svabhānu, Phālguṇa, śu. 2, Sun-day, Uttarā-bhādra, Śubhayōga, Bālavākara-ṇa.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South-Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
Records the establishment by Mādyaya, the headman of Kōyammuttūru, of an agrahāra called Mādhavapura to the west of Ānemale, and the allotment of shares of land to several Brahmans residing therein.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/8 (page 6)
Placement
A resident of Milatti, Kalyan-drug taluk, Anantapur district.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1658, Nala, Kārt-tika, śu. 15, Sunday.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Do.
Edition
Do.
Remarks
Registers the sale of the karaṇikam-right together with 3 villages, Varle, Puli-Timmāreḍḍipalle and Kāparlapalle by Subayya (Subbayya) and Apakeṇḍaya in a partition between themselves, to a certain Veṅkaṭagiriyappa, in return for 250 varāhas which they had borrowed from him.
ARIE/1927-1928/A/1927-28/9 (page 6)
Placement
Mr. M.Somasekhara Sarma of the ‘Bhārati’ Office, Madras.
Dynasty
Eastern Gaṅga.
King
Dēvēndravarman
Date
Śaka 1103
Language
Sanskrit in Nāgarī
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
…
Remarks
Written in very faulty Sanskrit. Records the grant of the village Rēviṇiji in Pañcha-vishaya to Nārāyaṇa, son of Rēvaṇa-Nāyaka and to Aitama-Śōmayā[ji], by Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Rāṇaka Śrī-Dharma-Khēḍi, son of Śrī-Bhīma-Khēḍi, who is described as a Paramamāhēśvara and Pañ-chavishayādhipati, and who belonged to the Kadamba family. (Published by Mr. Sarma in the Bhārati, Vol. VII.)

ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions copied in 1927-28/1927-28/5 (page 7)
Placement
On the same stone
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1150, Āshā-ḍha, śu. pāḍyami, Monday.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Registers the grant of 50 inpayeḍlu by several individuals for a perpetual lamp in the temple of Pālēśvara. The shepherds who were to receive the sheep and measure out the ghee were also granted some land for their mainte-nance.

NELLORE DISTRICT


NELLORE TALUK


ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions copied in 1927-28/1927-28/6 (page 7)
Placement
Kodur.--On a stone planted in a street.
Dynasty
Vijayanagara
King
[Śrīra]ṅgarāya-Mahārāya, ‘ruling from Penugoṇḍa’.
Date
Śaka 1567, Pārthi-va...., śu....
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Registers the settlement, as fixed by Rāvula-Veṅkaṭādri, of the mēras (proportions) due from the village in the Sariyapalli-sīma, for the upkeep of tanks. The sīma had been granted on amaram tenure to Rāvula-Muddukṛish-ṇappa-Nāyanivāru. (Same as No. 33, Nellore taluk of Butter worth's Nellore Inscriptions).

KURNOOL DISTRICT


NANDIKOTKUR TALUK


ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions copied in 1927-28/1927-28/9 (page 7)
Placement
Sivapuram.--On a stone plant-ed in front of the Mallēśvara temple.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Bhuvanaikamalladēva
Date
Śaka 991, Saumya, Āshāḍha, .. Tuesday, solar eclipse.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Registers a grant of land by the king at the request of his queens Rēvaladēvī and Mailaladēvī to Surēśvara-Paṇḍita, the disciple of Gaṅgarāśi-Bhaṭṭāraka, the āchārya of the Mosaṅgi Brahmēśvara temple, who is referred to as a follower of the Kāḷāmukha-samaya and gets a number of attributes of that creed.
ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions copied in 1927-28/1927-28/10 (page 7)
Placement
On another stone planted in the same temple.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Chāḷukya-Vikrama year 33, Sarva-[dhāri], Phālgu-ṇa, śu. 5, Vaḍḍa-vāra.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Registers a grant of land by Ārya-Paṇḍitadēva of Śivapura to two individuals for the renovation of the temple of Brahmēśvara. Mentions Mailaladēvī.
ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions copied in 1927-28/1927-28/11 (page 8)
Placement
On the same stone
Dynasty
Western Chālukya.
King
Trailōkyamalladēva
Date
Śaka[98]0, Viḷam-bi, Vaiśākha, paurṇami, Mon-day, Vyatīpāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Registers the grant of some lands in the village Śivapura in Kanne-nāḍu to god Ādibhairava of the western gate of the temple of Mallikārjuna, by queen Mailaladēvi and Ballavarasa, for the maintenance of a sattra for the ascetics visiting the temple.

ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions copied in 1927-28/1927-28/13 (page 8)
Placement
Bhairasamudram.--On a slab planted in front of the temple.
Dynasty
Vijayanagara.
King
Kṛishṇarāya-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1444, Chitra-bhānu, Pushya, śu. 10, Sunday, Makara-Saṅk-rānti.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Registers the grant of the village Bhairasamudram in Kugari-nāḍu, a subdivision of Kunduripi-sīma, as sarva-mānya for worship and offerings in the temple of Tiru-vēṅgaḷanātha of Vēmpalapariti by Kundurpi Narasa-Nāyaniṁgāru, who had the titles ‘Mahānāyaṁkāchārya, Bhāshadappuva-nāyaṁkara-gaṁḍa’ and ‘Marihokkare-kāva’, for the merit of his father Kundiripi Timma-Nāya-niṁgāru and Rāyasam Koṇḍamarasayya. The shares allotted to the sthānikas and the archakas of the temple are given at the end.

Telugu

Kannaḍa

ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions copied in 1927-28/1927-28/23 (page 9)
Placement
On a stone built into the south wall of the Raṅgasvāmin temple.
Dynasty
Vijayanagara
King
Śrīraṅgadēva-Mahārāya, ‘ruling from Penugoṇḍa.’
Date
Śaka 1513, Sva-bhānu (wrong), [Māgha], śu. 3, [Thursday].
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Seems to record a grant of land by the king to the temple of Śrīraṅganāthadēva at Eṟaguḍi surnamed Śrīraṅga-nāthasamudra in Vēparāla-veṇṭe, a sub-division of Rāya-durga-rājya, on the representation of several learned men of the village who gave him an account of the foundation of an agrahāra called Śrīraṅgasamudra by a certain Śrīraṅga, son of Tirumalanātha in the time of Kṛishṇa-dēva-Mahārāya and the construction of the temple men-tioned above.

Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Pratāpa Chakravartin Trailōkyamalla-dēva.
Date
7th year, Dhātu, Mārgaśira, śu. 13, Monday, Vyatī-pāta, Uttarāyaṇa-saṁkramaṇa.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Mentions a certain Daṇḍanāyaka Duggimayya who made a gift of land after purchasing it from a certain Gāmuṇḍa. Registers grants of land made by Jōga-Gāmuṇḍa and other local men to the tank called Vi[di]geyakeṟe. Also states that carpenters, blacksmiths, etc., offered their free services to the tank.

Kannaḍa
Remarks
Damaged. Seems to register a gift of land by a certain Nāyaka to the temple of Svayambhu-liṁga.

ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions of the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1927-28/1927-28/92 (page 27)
Placement
On a slab set up in the same place
Dynasty
Do.
King
Traiḷōkyamalladēva
Date
Śaka 970, Sarvva-dhāri, Vaiśākha, ....
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Mutilated and damaged. Seems to register a gift to some ascetics while Mahāsāmantādhipati Dāsarasa was administering Sirivura and while his father Mahāsāmantā-dhipati Mā[di]ṇayya was governing ‘five villages’ in Māsiyavāḍi--140.

ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions of the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1927-28/1927-28/217 (page 32)

…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Damaged and incomplete. Praises a certain person Māvidē[va*] as the devotee of (the god) Sōmēśvara, as a svāmihita (loyal to his master) and as the crest-jewel of the three worlds and refers to the Agastya-Puḻpagiri.
ARIE/1927-1928/Stone inscriptions of the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1927-28/1927-28/218 (page 32)
Placement
In the same place
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 955, Śrī-mukha, Āśvayuja, śu. 5, Sunday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records the consecration of the god Mallikārjuna at Agastya-Pushpagiri, to the south of (the temple of) Bhūtēśvara, by Kaṁchey[a]chāvayya. Refers also to the Pāpanāśatīrtha, Vishṇupāda and Rudrapāda.

Remarks
Labels such as ‘Bhīshma’, ‘Bhārata-yuddha’, ‘Arjuna’, etc., engraved under the scenes from the Mahābhārata sculptured on the pillar. See Cousens, Chalukyan Archi-tecture, 1926, p. 65, pl. XLIV.
